sudo tee /srv/iga-project/data/midpoint/scripts/SearchScript.groovy > /dev/null << 'EOF'
import groovy.json.JsonSlurper
import org.apache.http.client.methods.HttpGet
import org.apache.http.impl.client.HttpClients
import org.apache.http.util.EntityUtils

def client = HttpClients.createDefault()
def request = new HttpGet("http://xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx:8000/employees")
request.setHeader("X-API-KEY", "Fiqueok-Security-Token-2026")
request.setHeader("Accept", "application/json")

def response = client.execute(request)
def body = EntityUtils.toString(response.getEntity())
client.close()

def slurper = new JsonSlurper()
def employees = slurper.parseText(body)

employees.each { emp ->
    def co = handler.newConnectorObject()
    co.setObjectClass(new ObjectClass("AccountObjectClass"))
    co.setUid(emp.emp_number?.toString())
    co.setName(emp.emp_number?.toString())
    if (emp.employee_id) co.addAttribute("employee_id", emp.employee_id)
    if (emp.first_name) co.addAttribute("first_name", emp.first_name)
    if (emp.last_name) co.addAttribute("last_name", emp.last_name)
    if (emp.employment_status) co.addAttribute("employment_status", emp.employment_status)
    handler.handle(co.build())
}
EOF

SearchScript.groovy
paulo@iga-gf-02:/srv/iga-project/data/midpoint/scripts$ cat SearchScript.groovy
import groovy.json.JsonSlurper
import org.apache.http.client.methods.HttpGet
import org.apache.http.impl.client.HttpClients
import org.apache.http.util.EntityUtils

def client = HttpClients.createDefault()
def request = new HttpGet("http://xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx:8000/employees")
request.setHeader("X-API-KEY", "Fiqueok-Security-Token-2026")
request.setHeader("Accept", "application/json")

def response = client.execute(request)
def body = EntityUtils.toString(response.getEntity())
client.close()

def slurper = new JsonSlurper()
def employees = slurper.parseText(body)

employees.each { emp ->
    def co = handler.newConnectorObject()
    co.setObjectClass(new ObjectClass("AccountObjectClass"))
    co.setUid(emp.emp_number?.toString())
    co.setName(emp.emp_number?.toString())
    if (emp.employee_id) co.addAttribute("employee_id", emp.employee_id)
    if (emp.first_name) co.addAttribute("first_name", emp.first_name)
    if (emp.last_name) co.addAttribute("last_name", emp.last_name)
    if (emp.employment_status) co.addAttribute("employment_status", emp.employment_status)
    handler.handle(co.build())
}

import groovy.json.JsonSlurper
import org.apache.http.client.methods.HttpGet
import org.apache.http.impl.client.HttpClients
import org.apache.http.util.EntityUtils
import org.identityconnectors.framework.common.objects.ConnectorObjectBuilder
import org.identityconnectors.framework.common.objects.ObjectClass
import org.identityconnectors.framework.common.objects.AttributeBuilder
import org.identityconnectors.framework.common.objects.Name
import org.identityconnectors.framework.common.objects.Uid

def httpClient = HttpClients.createDefault()
def get = new HttpGet("http://xxx.xxx.xxx.xxx:8000/employees")
get.setHeader("X-API-KEY", "Fiqueok-Security-Token-2026")
get.setHeader("Accept", "application/json")

def response = httpClient.execute(get)
def body = EntityUtils.toString(response.getEntity(), "UTF-8")
httpClient.close()

def parser = new JsonSlurper()
def list = parser.parseText(body)

list.each { emp ->
    def builder = new ConnectorObjectBuilder()
    builder.setObjectClass(ObjectClass.ACCOUNT)
    builder.setUid(new Uid(emp.emp_number.toString()))
    builder.setName(new Name(emp.emp_number.toString()))
    if (emp.employee_id) builder.addAttribute(AttributeBuilder.build("employee_id", emp.employee_id.toString()))
    if (emp.first_name)  builder.addAttribute(AttributeBuilder.build("first_name",  emp.first_name.toString()))
    if (emp.last_name)   builder.addAttribute(AttributeBuilder.build("last_name",   emp.last_name.toString()))
    if (emp.employment_status) builder.addAttribute(AttributeBuilder.build("employment_status", emp.employment_status.toString()))
    handler.handle(builder.build())
}
EOF
